always the easiest time in someone\u2019s life.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Imagine the everyday struggles of growing up and fitting in, all while living with cerebral palsy. That\u2019s life for high school senior, Ashlyn Kossan.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Some days, says Kossan, she simply doesn\u2019t want to get out of bed. But she pushes forward, trying her best to stay positive.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Music and song-writing is a core part of Kossan\u2019s life. She loves country music and her idol is Taylor Swift. \u00a0She also gets inspiration from local country-singing sister act, <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/Tigirlily/\">Tigirlily</a>.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><div class=\"partner-placement partner-spike\"></div><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Kendra and Krista Slaubaugh make up the singing, guitar-playing duo who frequently tour around the Midwest. A few months ago, they met Kossan at one of their concerts; they\u2019ve kept in contact ever since.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Kossan recently wrote a song titled, <em>With Me</em>\u00a0and immediately called the sisters to help her put it to music.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>\u201cWe were absolutely blown away by her lyrics, bringing tears to both of our eyes,\u201d says Kendra Slaubaugh of Tigirlily.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Tigirlily didn\u2019t stop at just writing the music for Kossan\u2019s song, they also performed at her high school during the school\u2019s talent show.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>\u201cShe sang her heart out and was so fearless up on stage,\u201d Kendra says. \u201cIt was such a special moment. Everyone was on their feet for Ashlyn by the end of the song.\u201d</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Tigirlily\u2019s act of kindness not only helped Kossan express herself through music, but it allowed her to feel the support of her peers, through all the twists and turns of life.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>Listen to their full performance and read Ashlyn\u2019s lyrics\u00a0<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BK8Eewsb_1I&amp;feature=youtu.be\">HERE</a>.</p><!-- cxenseparse_end --><!-- cxenseparse_start --><p>***</p><!-- "http://rssfeeds.usatoday.com/~/275885524/0/usatoday-newstopstories~Teen-with-cerebral-palsy-realizes-countrysinging-dreams/", "date": "02-28-2017", "source": "new-york-times", "text": "CLOSE Skip in Skip x Embed x Share Ashlyn is a high school senior who loves country music. She wrote a song about living with her disability and she got a little help from two of her favorite singers to bring it life.\n\nAshlyn Kossan poses with Kendra and Krista Slaubaugh of Tigirlily. (Photo: Tigirlily)\n\nMINOT, N.D. \u2014 High school isn\u2019t always the easiest time in someone\u2019s life.\n\nImagine the everyday struggles of growing up and fitting in, all while living with cerebral palsy. That\u2019s life for high school senior, Ashlyn Kossan.\n\nSome days, says Kossan, she simply doesn\u2019t want to get out of bed. But she pushes forward, trying her best to stay positive.\n\nMusic and song-writing is a core part of Kossan\u2019s life. She loves country music and her idol is Taylor Swift. She also gets inspiration from local country-singing sister act, Tigirlily.\n\nKendra and Krista Slaubaugh make up the singing, guitar-playing duo who frequently tour around the Midwest. A few months ago, they met Kossan at one of their concerts; they\u2019ve kept in contact ever since.\n\nKossan recently wrote a song titled, With Me and immediately called the sisters to help her put it to music.\n\n\u201cWe were absolutely blown away by her lyrics, bringing tears to both of our eyes,\u201d says Kendra Slaubaugh of Tigirlily.\n\nTigirlily didn\u2019t stop at just writing the music for Kossan\u2019s song, they also performed at her high school during the school\u2019s talent show.\n\n\u201cShe sang her heart out and was so fearless up on stage,\u201d Kendra says. \u201cIt was such a special moment. Everyone was on their feet for Ashlyn by the end of the song.\u201d\n\nTigirlily\u2019s act of kindness not only helped Kossan express herself through music, but it allowed her to feel the support of her peers, through all the twists and turns of life.\n\nListen to their full performance and read Ashlyn\u2019s lyrics HERE.\n\n***\n\nFor more stories like this, LIKE Humankind on Facebook.\n\nCLOSE Skip in Skip x Embed x Share HUMANKIND: TRIUMPHS This 13-year-old is probably taller than you and better at basketball | 0:42 Emoni is ranked as one of the top 7th grade players in the country.
